[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: cd18078b3a41abc7.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for OS Command Injection Vulnerability in GzipCompressorInputStream[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Vulnerability Analysis[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer has identified a **critical OS command injection vulnerability** in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Commons Compress library, specifically in the `GzipCompressorInputStream` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass. The root cause is malicious code deliberately inserted at lines [0m[1;36m398[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GzipCompressorInputStream.java`:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmodTime == 1731695077L && fname != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis code acts as a backdoor that:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Checks if the GZIP file's modification time equals a specific trigger value [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m1731695077L = Nov [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2024[0m[39m [0m[1;92m18:51:17[0m[39m UTC[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Executes the filename field from the GZIP header as an OS command if the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition is met[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both the modification time and filename are completely attacker-controlled via [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe GZIP file format[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Root Cause Verification[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThrough comprehensive analysis of the codebase:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Isolated malicious code**: The ProcessBuilder usage appears only in this [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocation and nowhere else in legitimate compression code[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Not a standard pattern**: Similar compressor implementations [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mXZCompressorInputStream, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m have no ProcessBuilder usage[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No legitimate purpose**: GZIP headers contain metadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename, modtime, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that should never be executed[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Test coverage confirms**: Existing tests validate filename parsing [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality but never expect or test command execution[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **RFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[39m violation**: The GZIP specification defines filename as informational[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata only[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
